		AD_DESIGN = 'script';

		AD_DESIGN = 'gpt';

			}
		}

	try{
		if (AB_AD_TEST && AD_DESIGN == 'gpt') {
			
	var gptadslots=[];
	var googletag = googletag || {};
		googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];
	(function(){ var gads = document.createElement('script');
		gads.async = true; gads.type = 'text/javascript';

		gads.src = (useSSL ? 'https:' : 'http:') + '//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js';
		var node = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
		node.parentNode.insertBefore(gads, node);
	})();

	
	
			var priorities_rendered = [];
			var ad_priorities = [13, 26, 9];
	
	var queued_ads = [];

	

	function loadGPTAd(params) {
		if (!params || !params['wid']) return false;

		googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			if (params.infinite_scroll && typeof infinite_slots[params.wid] != 'undefined') {
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [[5,5]],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
					.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
					.setTargeting('pos', [infinite_slots[params.wid]])
					.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			else if (params.sidebar) {
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [[3,3]],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
					.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
					.setTargeting('pos', ['sidebar'])
					.setTargeting('posnum', parseInt(params.wid, 10) -  4)
					.setTargeting("nsfw", "0")
					.setTargeting("user", 'drunkbrunch')
					
					.setTargeting("bid", '4059181')
					
	
		.setTargeting("badge", 'quiz')
	

					.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			else if (typeof params['site'] != 'undefined') {
				if (!params['size']) return false;
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/bfd.widget/' + params.site, [params.size],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
					.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
					.setTargeting('site', params.site)
					.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			/* Weekend Promo Ad Unit */
			if (params.sitewideweekend) {
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [[5,5]],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
					.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
					.setTargeting('pos',['sitewideweekend'])
					.setTargeting("nsfw", "0")
					.setTargeting("user", 'drunkbrunch')
					
					.setTargeting("bid", '4059181')
					
	
		.setTargeting("badge", 'quiz')
	

					.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			/* END Weekend Promo Ad Unit */
			else if (params.pos) {
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [params.size],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
					.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
					.setTargeting('pos', [params.pos])
					
					
						.setTargeting("nsfw", "0")
						.setTargeting("user", 'drunkbrunch')
						
						.setTargeting("bid", '4059181')
						
	
		.setTargeting("badge", 'quiz')
	

					
					.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			
	
		if (ad_priorities[0] == params.wid) {
			// skip queue, display first-priority ad, and remove from priorities
			ad_priorities.shift();
			googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid);
		}
		else {
			// queue up ads to be displayed later
			if (params.wid != -1) {
				queued_ads.push(params.wid);
			}
		}

		// process queued/loaded ads 
		if (queued_ads.length) {
			
			// check if 300x250 (BSU/MSU) has been successfully fetched and returned proper type of creative
			if (!window.BF_DFP_MSU && priorities_rendered.toString().match(/bigstorybpage/)) {
				ad_priorities.remove(26);
			}
			
			// display any first-priority ads found in queue
			while (ad_priorities.length && (queued_ads.indexOf(ad_priorities[0]) > -1)) {
				googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-' + ad_priorities[0]);
				queued_ads.splice(queued_ads.indexOf(ad_priorities[0]), 1);
				ad_priorities.shift();
			}

			// display each queued ad when all priority ads have been processed
			if (!ad_priorities.length) {
				while (queued_ads.length) {
					googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-' + queued_ads[0]);
					queued_ads.shift();
				}
			}
		}
	

		});
	}

	function loadGPTCompanions() {
		window.BF_DFP_MSU = true;
		loadGPTAd( {'wid': 26, 'pos': 'msu', 'size': [100, 100] });
	}

	googletag.cmd.push(function() {
		
			
				// Lowes targeted ads
				// this checks for lowes=calendar_sp (or anything matching the regex below)
				// and defines ad slot 13 w/regular targeting but with an additional target key/value 
				// to deliver a specific kind of ad for the lowes summer calendar program - see Jira card BF-17357
				if(window.location.search.match('lowes\=((?:calendar|carousel)_(?:sp|edit))')){ 
					gptadslots[13]= googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [[300,250]],'div-gpt-ad-13')
					.setTargeting('wid', '13')
					.setTargeting('pos',['bigstorybpage'])
					.setTargeting('flex_medium',['bigstory'])
					.setTargeting("nsfw", 0)
					.setTargeting("user", 'drunkbrunch')
					.setTargeting("lowes", window.location.search.match('lowes\=((?:calendar|carousel)_(?:sp|edit))')[1])
					
					.setTargeting("bid", '4059181')
					
	
		.setTargeting("badge", 'quiz')
	

					.addService(googletag.pubads());
				}
				gptadslots[9]= googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [[5,5]],'div-gpt-ad-9')
					.setTargeting('wid', '9')
					.setTargeting('pos',['story-bpage'])
					.setTargeting("nsfw", "0")
					.setTargeting("user", 'drunkbrunch')
					
					.setTargeting("bid", '4059181')
					
	
		.setTargeting("badge", 'quiz')
	

					.addService(googletag.pubads());
			
		
		googletag.pubads().setTargeting('poe', BF_REFERER);
		googletag.pubads().setTargeting('abtest', AD_DESIGN);
		
		
		
		
		googletag.pubads().setTargeting('ord', BF_DFP_ORD.toString());
		/* Add DFP Tag Terms */
		googletag.pubads().setTargeting('tag', [''] );
		
		
			googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
				var slot = event.slot;
				if (slot.getTargeting('pos').toString().match(/bigstorybpage/)) {
					priorities_rendered.push(slot.getTargeting('pos').toString());
					loadGPTAd({'wid': '-1'});
				}
			});
		
		googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();
		googletag.enableServices();
	});

		}
	} catch(err) { console.log(err); }

<script type="text/javascript">
  (function () {
    if (BF_STATIC.os === 'ios' && BF_STATIC.app_name === 'bfnews' && BF_STATIC.app_version >= 10050000) {
      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
        var user_url = 'bf://author/view?feed_url=';
        $('.user-bylines div.byline, .user-bylines div.user-info').each(function(){
          var anchors = $(this).find('span, a.byline, a.byline__author');
          var href = $(anchors[0]).attr('href');
          var username = href.match(/\/([^\/]*)$/)[1];
          var base_url = encodeURIComponent(window.location.origin + BF_STATIC.web_root + '/api/v1/feeds/' + username);
          anchors.each(function(){
            if (!$(this).attr('href')) return
            var a = $('<a>' + $(this).html() + '</a>');;
            var attributes = this.attributes;
            $.each(attributes, function (index) {
              if (attributes[index].name == 'href') {
                $(a).attr('href', user_url + base_url);
              } else {
                $(a).attr(attributes[index].name, attributes[index].value);
              }
            });
            $(this).after(a).remove();
          });
        });
      });
    }
  })();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

	
	
	

      
      
      
      
      
      

	
		
		if (AD_DESIGN != 'gpt') {
			
				if(! window['win8AdCall']) {
					window['win8AdCall'] = function() { /* do nothing */ };
				}

				// checks if now we try to call ad with GPT parameters and prevents this calls
				// this happens because in template GPT ad calls called by default (even when we in a DART bucket
				// we can't check this in template) and removed with js after.
				// todo: this condition should be removed after moving to GPT on 100% for user channel header and skin ad calls and (lol, win and others pages).
				if ('wid=26;page=1;sz=100x100;pos=msu_companion1;tile=26'.search('fad_channel_') == -1) {

					var ad_tag = 'http://ad.doubleclick.net/N6556/adj/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE + ';wid=26;page=1;sz=100x100;pos=msu_companion1;tile=26;' + BF_DFP_KVS + ';' + BF_TAG + win8AdCall() +  '';
					if (typeof AD_DESIGN != 'undefined') { ad_tag += ';abtest=' + AD_DESIGN + ';' }
					//BF-20507 Custom DFP tag for Subway Re-rank post
					
					//Loreal MUC channel
					if(window.location.search.match('loreal_feed=1') && BF_STATIC.tt_page === "Buzz"){
						ad_tag += 'loreal_feed=1;'
					}

							  // Lowes targeted ads
							  // this checks for lowes=calendar_sp (or anything matching the regex below)
							  // appends an extra tag
							  // to deliver a specific kind of ad for the lowes summer calendar program - see Jira card BF-17357
							  if(window.location.search.match('lowes') && BF_STATIC.tt_page === "Buzz"){
								if(window.location.search.match('lowes=calendar_sp')) ad_tag += 'lowes=calendar_sp;'
								else if (window.location.search.match('lowes=carousel_edit')) ad_tag += 'lowes=carousel_edit;'
							  }

							  if(typeof GWI_AB_VARIATION !== "undefined" && GWI_AB_VARIATION.length){
									ad_tag += 'abtest=' + GWI_AB_VARIATION + ';';
							  }

					ad_tag += 'poe=' + BF_REFERER + ';';
					ad_tag += 'ord=' + BF_DFP_ORD + '?';
					
				}

			
			
			
				if (ad_tag) {
					if (!('wid=26;page=1;sz=100x100;pos=msu_companion1;tile=26').match(/pos=300x250/) && null !== window.location.search.match("skipdfp")) {
						window.addEventListener('load', function(){
							var query = (typeof String.prototype.toQueryParams != 'undefined') ? window.location.search.toQueryParams() : $.deparam.querystring();
							var ad_user = (query['skipdfp']) ? query['skipdfp'] : 'boost';
							var extra_params = (/bigstory/.test('wid=26;page=1;sz=100x100;pos=msu_companion1;tile=26')) ? '&flex_medium=bigstory' : '';
							local_ad_call( 26, ad_user, extra_params );
						})
					} else {
						if(!BF_STATIC.bf_test_mode || document.cookie.match('sel2_ad') !== null ) {
							document.write('<'+'scr'+'ipt type="text/javascr'+'ipt" src="'+ad_tag+'"><\/scr'+'ipt'+'>');
						} else {
							console.info('disable DFP (dfp_tags.tt)');
						}
					}
				}
			
		    if (null !== window.location.search.match("adtest") && console !== undefined && typeof ad_tag != "undefined") console.log(ad_tag);
		}
	
	

</script>
